Local Romney event cracks $1 million, breaks $750k Bush record

John Ellis | Thursday, May 31, 2012 at 4:37pm

It's pretty much official: Presumptive Republican presidential nominee Mitt Romney raked in more than $1 million at a Wednesday lunch fundraiser at the Sanger-area home of prominent west-side rancher John Harris and his wife Carole.

It's the first time a Valley fundraiser has hit the $1 million mark, and is the largest area fundraiser ever, local political watchers from both parties said. The event shattered the $750,000 raised in October 2003 at the Fresno Convention Center by President George W. Bush.

The crowd at the Romney event was overwhelmingly from the Valley's agricultural community, and preceded a similar Romney event in Bakersfield later on Wednesday, which also hit the $1 million mark.

Longtime Sacramento-based Republican fundraiser Wendy Warfield spearheaded both events.

The event at Harris' home was only for the richest of the local rich, and is likely the last time Romney will hit up the Valley for money -- at least during this election cycle.

Through March, he had raised more than $280,000 from donors in the region. Add thismillion-plus from the Harris event, and the local ATM machine is pretty much dried up, local Republicans and Democrats agreed.

Local Romney event cracks $1 million, breaks $750k Bush record

John Ellis | Thursday, May 31, 2012 at 4:37pm

It's pretty much official: Presumptive Republican presidential nominee Mitt Romney raked in more than $1 million at a Wednesday lunch fundraiser at the Sanger-area home of prominent west-side rancher John Harris and his wife Carole.

It's the first time a Valley fundraiser has hit the $1 million mark, and is the largest area fundraiser ever, local political watchers from both parties said. The event shattered the $750,000 raised in October 2003 at the Fresno Convention Center by President George W. Bush.

The crowd at the Romney event was overwhelmingly from the Valley's agricultural community, and preceded a similar Romney event in Bakersfield later on Wednesday, which also hit the $1 million mark.

Longtime Sacramento-based Republican fundraiser Wendy Warfield spearheaded both events.

The event at Harris' home was only for the richest of the local rich, and is likely the last time Romney will hit up the Valley for money -- at least during this election cycle.

Through March, he had raised more than $280,000 from donors in the region. Add thismillion-plus from the Harris event, and the local ATM machine is pretty much dried up, local Republicans and Democrats agreed.

Buffalo Sabres Jackie Style with Single Ring Base

FedEx Shipping Options

FedEx ground, FedEx 2 Day, FedEx standard overnight. Please check the fedex website http://www.fedex.com/us/ for service details for your destination zip code

Truck Shipping Options for Heavy Items:

Â Â 

Curb Side Delivery

This is our basic delivery option for heavy shipments and can also be refered to as "back of truck": or "self service". We typically ship from our warehouse, or the manufacturers warehouse, within 2 to 4 days of when the order is placed. Transit times vary by the delivery location. The delivery will be curbside, meaning the driver will stop at the closet curb near the delivery location and the driver will bring the item(s) to the rear of the truck. At that threshold it becomesÂ the recipients obligation to get the item off of the truck and to the final set up location. Drivers do help sometimes, but they are NOT obligated to. Please make sure that you have sufficient help at receipt to handle your item.

Curb Side Delivery with Liftgate

This delivery option is the same as curbside except the truck is equipped with a lift gate that will lower the item to the ground. At thatÂ point, the customers obligations will be the same as basic curb side. Please understand that for extreme length products the liftgate option may be of limited value and the customer may still need to assist in getting the item(s) to ground level.

Inside Delivery any Room

Truck Shipping Options for Heavy Items:

Â Â 

Curb Side Delivery

This is our basic delivery option for heavy shipments and can also be refered to as "back of truck": or "self service". We typically ship from our warehouse, or the manufacturers warehouse, within 2 to 4 days of when the order is placed. Transit times vary by the delivery location. The delivery will be curbside, meaning the driver will stop at the closet curb near the delivery location and the driver will bring the item(s) to the rear of the truck. At that threshold it becomesÂ the recipients obligation to get the item off of the truck and to the final set up location. Drivers do help sometimes, but they are NOT obligated to. Please make sure that you have sufficient help at receipt to handle your item.

Curb Side Delivery with Liftgate

This delivery option is the same as curbside except the truck is equipped with a lift gate that will lower the item to the ground. At thatÂ point, the customers obligations will be the same as basic curb side. Please understand that for extreme length products the liftgate option may be of limited value and the customer may still need to assist in getting the item(s) to ground level.
